This website includes analyses to assess the performance of mr.mash.

Results for meeting on 03/30/2020.

  • Assessment of prediction accuracy.
  • Assessment of convergence.

Results for meeting on 04/16/2020. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different options in the following simulation scenarios:

  • Independent predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Independent predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.

Results for meeting on 04/30/2020. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different options in the following simulation scenarios:

  • Independent predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Independent predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Highly correlated predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Highly correlated predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.

Results for meeting on 05/27/2020. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different options against the multivariate versions of LASSO, Elastic Net, and Ridge regression in the following simulation scenarios:

  • Independent predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Independent predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Correlated predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Highly correlated predictors, shared effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Highly correlated predictors, independent effects, lowly correlated residuals.
  • Case study with only two causal responses out of five total.

Results for meeting on 09/29/2020. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different prior specifications against the multivariate versions of LASSO, Elastic Net, and Ridge regression in GTEx-like scenarios:

  • Three scenarios for predictors correlation, two blocks of responses (shared effects within block), independent residuals.
  • Independent predictors, three causal responses (shared effects) out of ten, independent residuals.

Results for meeting on 10/23/2020. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different prior specifications against the multivariate version of LASSO, UTMOST, and univariate Elastic Net in simulations based on GTEx v8 genotypes:

  • One causal response out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Three causal responses (with shared effects) out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Two blocks of responses (shared effects within block), independent residuals.
  • Shared effects, independent residuals.
  • Indpendent effects, independent residuals.

Results for meeting on 01/08/2021. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different prior specifications against the multivariate version of LASSO, UTMOST, and univariate Elastic Net in simulations based on GTEx v8 genotypes with truly independent replicates:

  • One causal response out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Three causal responses (with shared effects) out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Two blocks of responses (shared effects within block), independent residuals.
  • Shared effects, independent residuals.
  • Indpendent effects, independent residuals.

Results for meeting on 03/29/2021. Assessment of prediction accuracy and run time of mr.mash with different prior specifications against UTMOST, and univariate Elastic Net in simulations based on GTEx v8 genotypes with truly independent replicates and missing values in Y:

  • One causal response out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Three causal responses (with shared effects) out of ten, independent residuals.
  • Two blocks of responses (shared effects within block), independent residuals.
  • Shared effects, independent residuals.
  • Indpendent effects, independent residuals.

Other investigations:

  • Case study with dense scenarios.
  • Case study with dense scenarios and larger sample size.
  • Case study with dense scenarios and univariate analysis.
  • mash vs mr.mash.
  • Case study with only two causal responses out of six total.
  • Case study with larger number of conditions.
